<section class="pi-item pi-group pi-border-color pi-collapse pi-collapse-open">
<table class="pi-horizontal-group pi-horizontal-group-no-labels">
<caption class="pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-secondary-background pi-item-spacing">Related Wikis</caption>

<td class="pi-horizontal-group-item pi-data-value pi-font pi-border-color pi-item-spacing" data-source="related"><p><a class="extiw" href="https://shinee.fandom.com/wiki/Taemin" title="w:c:shinee:Taemin">SHINee Wiki</a> • <a class="extiw" href="https://superm.fandom.com/wiki/Taemin" title="w:c:superm:Taemin">SuperM Wiki</a> • <a class="extiw" href="https://smtown.fandom.com/wiki/Taemin" title="w:c:smtown:Taemin">SMTown Wiki</a></p></td>

<b>Taemin</b> (Korean: 태민; Japanese: テミン) is a South Korean singer-songwriter and actor under <a href="/wiki/BPM_Entertainment" title="BPM Entertainment">BPM Entertainment</a>. He is the maknae of the boy group <a href="/wiki/SHINee" title="SHINee">SHINee</a> and a member of the supergroup <a href="/wiki/SuperM" title="SuperM">SuperM</a>.
</p><p>He made his solo debut on August 18, 2014 with the mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Ace_(Taemin)" title="Ace (Taemin)">Ace</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career">Career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2008:_Debut_with_SHINee">2008: Debut with SHINee</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On May 25, 2008, he debuted as a member of <a href="/wiki/SHINee" title="SHINee">SHINee</a> with the group's first mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Replay_(SHINee)" title="Replay (SHINee)">Replay</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2014:_Solo_debut_with_Ace">2014: Solo debut with <i>Ace</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>He was the first SHINee member to make his debut as a solo artist on August 18, 2014 with his first mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Ace_(Taemin)" title="Ace (Taemin)">Ace</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2019:_Debut_with_SuperM">2019: Debut with SuperM</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On August 4, 2019, he was revealed as a member of the supergroup <a href="/wiki/SuperM" title="SuperM">SuperM</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The group debuted on October 4 with their <a href="/wiki/SuperM_(album)" title="SuperM (album)">self-titled mini album</a>.
</p>
<h3><span id="2024:_Departure_from_SM_Entertainment.2C_signing_with_BPM.2C_Eternal"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2024:_Departure_from_SM_Entertainment,_signing_with_BPM,_Eternal">2024: Departure from SM Entertainment, signing with BPM, <i>Eternal</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On March 5, 2024, it was announced that Taemin's contract with SM Entertainment will be expiring in March. It was reported that he will not renew and may be signing with <a href="/wiki/BPM_Entertainment" title="BPM Entertainment">BPM Entertainment</a> to manage his solo activities. In response, BPM stated that nothing has been decided as of yet.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The next day, Taemin personally announced that he is leaving SM Entertainment.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On April 1, BPM Entertainment officially announced that they had signed an exclusive contract with Taemin.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On the last date of the <span class="new" data-uncrawlable-url="L3dpa2kvMjAyNF9UYWVtaW5fRmFubWVldGluZ18lMjdOZXZlci1OZXZlciUyNz9hY3Rpb249ZWRpdCZyZWRsaW5rPTE=" title="2024 Taemin Fanmeeting 'Never-Never' (page does not exist)">2024 Taemin Fanmeeting [Never-Never]</span>, it was revealed that Taemin will release his fifth mini album in August before going on a world tour.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On July 29, he released a teaser for <i><a href="/wiki/Eternal_(Taemin)" title="Eternal (Taemin)">Eternal</a></i>, set for release on August 19.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In March 2011, he transferred from Chungdam High School to Hanlim Multi Arts School to accommodate for <a href="/wiki/SHINee" title="SHINee">SHINee</a>'s Japanese promotions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>8<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> He graduated on February 10, 2012, but was unable to attend the ceremony due to group promotions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>9<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>For college, he attended Myongji University where he majored in Musical and Film.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Military_service">Military service</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On April 19, 2021, Taemin revealed he will be the final member of SHINee to enlist as a member of the military band on May 31.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>  On January 14, 2022, it was announced that Taemin would finish the rest of his military service as a public service worker due to worsening symptoms of depression, anxiety and panic disorder.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> He was discharged on April 4, 2023.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>13<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Discography">Discography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Japanese">Japanese</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FTaemin_%28SHINee%29%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>He is a Roman Catholic; his baptismal name is Francesco.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>26<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>He is close friends with <a href="/wiki/Kai_(EXO)" title="Kai (EXO)">Kai</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Timoteo" title="Timoteo">Timoteo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ha_Sung_Woon" title="Ha Sung Woon">Ha Sung Woon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jimin_(BTS)" title="Jimin (BTS)">Jimin</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ravi" title="Ravi">Ravi</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:0_27-0"><a href="#cite_note-:0-27"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>27<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
<ul><li>The group is often called the "Friendship Parkas Squad" or the "Parka Squad" because they all have matching parkas.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:0_27-1"><a href="#cite_note-:0-27"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>27<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>He is a huge fan of Sia and Michael Jackson.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>28<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>29<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
<ul><li>It was precisely Michael Jackson who made Taemin fall in love with dance: according to him, his love for dance came after watching a show of the King of Pop when he was studying in the sixth grade.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>30<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>He's not good at cooking.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>31<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>He purchased a house for his parents.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>32<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>His favorite color is purple.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:1_33-0"><a href="#cite_note-:1-33"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>33<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>He doesn't like cucumbers.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:1_33-1"><a href="#cite_note-:1-33"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>33<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>He has a grey and white cat named Kkoong and a white cat named Ddaengie.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>34<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>35<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>36<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
<ul><li>His family also has two dogs named Adam and Eve whom he got before he debuted.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>37<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></li></ul></li></ul>
